#---------------------------------------------------------------------------
#
# Use CM_CVCELL_COMMAND to point to this file
#
#---------------------------------------------------------------------------
# Available commands:
#---------------------------------------------------------------------------
#
#
# CELL_LIBRARY,cell_lib_path		- Sets the default cell library
#
#
# CELLSUB,oldcellname,newcellname,.. - replaces cell instance(s)
#
# This can be followed by "LIB, celllibraryname," to define a cell library for the replacement other than the default 
#
#
# This can then be followed by any number of cell commands
# eg: CELLSUB,oldcellname,newcellname, SCALE,10, ORDER,GENERAL, SPLIT,-1, DRAWINGNUM,4, NUMFIELDS,1, FILL,GENERAL
# 
#
# Note: leading and trailing spaces are ignored
# Note Don't use quote marks
#
#---------------------------------------------------------------------------
